<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roef.html>roef</a> (79969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roef.html>roef</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ruof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrōfą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roef.html>roef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roef.html>roeven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roef.html>roefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cabin</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on a boat</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tapering <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> of a coffin, with a triangular cross-section</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> triangular frame placed <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> a coffin or <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>, on which a cloth <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> laid</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">roeyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ruoien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rōaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁reh₁-</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roekeloos.html>roekeloos</a> (8253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the now obsolete Dutch verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeken.html>roeken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to care, to worry (about)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ruchlos</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reckless</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roekeloos.html>roekeloos</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roekeloos.html>roekelozer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roekeloos.html>roekeloos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">roekeloost</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reckless</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***roeken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roeken.html>roeken</a> (124606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeken.html>roeken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ruoken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rōkijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeken.html>roeken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay attention to, to heed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to care about, to worry about</li></ol>

***roem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roem.html>roem</a> (5590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roem.html>roem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boasting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ruom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrōmaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noise, shouting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related also to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrōþiz</i> with a change to a dental <a href = vnd.unilang:consonant.html>consonant</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>Ie</a> origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ruhm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hrēmiġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">exultant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>glory (honour and valour)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roepen.html>roepen</a> (1831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roepen.html>roepen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ruopan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrōpaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roepen.html>roepen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cry, shout</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, summon, invite etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">shout</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brullen.html>brullen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulderen.html>bulderen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuwen.html>schreeuwen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></span></li></ul>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***roer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a> (5678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a contraction of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roeder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">roeder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ruother</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rōþrą</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ruder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rudder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A boat's wheel</li>
<li>A rudder, device to steer a vessel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(used absolutely, with the definite article: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a></b>)</i> control
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a> — <i>to have (situation, etc.) under control</i>, <i>to be in charge</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roer.html>roertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> light <a href = vnd.unilang:musket.html>musket</a>, matchlock gun
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vuurroer</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stir, scramble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">egg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rührei</i>.

***roeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a> (14100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ruoren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrōzijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeren.html>roeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stir, scramble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> touch, move (to cause emotion)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play an instrument
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>Wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:virtuoos.html>virtuoos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:roerde.html>roerde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iedereen.html>iedereen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tranen.html>tranen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geroerd.html>geroerd</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When the virtuoso <b>played</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompet</a>, everyone <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>moved</b> to <a href = vnd.unilang:tears.html>tears</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***roest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a> (13536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rusta-</i>. The vowel <i><a href = vnd.unilang:oe.html>oe</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to an irregular sound development.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
See English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">result of oxidation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-, second- and third-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roesten.html>roesten</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roesten.html>roesten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Froom <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">roost</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roestig.html>roestig</a> (19560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roest.html>roest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***roger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>roger</a> (2301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>Roger</a></i>, used circa 1940 in UK and US military communication to represent "<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>" when spelling out a word. "<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the first letter in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">received</i>, used to acknowledge understanding a message. "<a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>Roger</a>" for "received" in <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> usage in air traffic radio parlance by 1950.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>roger</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">radio telecommunications</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Received <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used in radio communications to acknowledge that a message <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> received and understood</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1950</b> May,  <cite>Flying Magazine</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ch/books?id=bJ1HBQf26b0Camp;pg=PA46">[1]</a></sup>, page 46:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Pilot: CESSNA TWO THREE FOUR | <b><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>Roger</a></b> | OUT.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>roger</a> that</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">Hrotger</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shelta" class="extiw" title="w:Shelta">Shelta</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sth"><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>roger</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>roger</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">rogers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rogering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rogered</b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, to have sexual intercourse with (someone), especially in a rough manner.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To have sexual intercourse.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to have sexual intercourse with someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bone</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">knob</span>; see also Thesaurus:copulate with</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rogge.html>rogge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*roggo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*roggō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ruggô</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Rogg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:rogge.html>rogge</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:roggen.html>Roggen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rye</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***roken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a> (1528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rôken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke (a tobacco product, another drug, a surrogate)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sigaret.html>sigaret</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b>are smoking</b> a cigarette.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">But I <b>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> smoke</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>Vroeger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> in zeemansbuurten <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> opium <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerookt.html>gerookt</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">People used to <b>smoke</b> a lot of opium in the sailors' <a href = vnd.unilang:districts.html>districts</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke, to produce smoke
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rookte.html>rookte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:enorm.html>enorm</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The engine <b>produced</b> a great amount of <b>smoke</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***rol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a> (1266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollen.html>rolle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">role</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollen.html>rollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rolletje.html>rolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>role, function (as in actions or tasks that a person or a group <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> expected to perform)</li>
<li>roll <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">cylindrical object, often used as a rolling part</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> role, character</li></ol>

***rolluik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rolluik.html>rolluik</a> (48577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollen.html>rollen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luik.html>luik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shutter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roll, scroll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luik.html>luik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shutter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rommelig.html>rommelig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rommeliger.html>rommeliger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">rommeligst</b>)

<ol><li>messy, disorderly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
